<div style="position:absolute;left:0;top:0"><img alt="Circle frame.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/18/Circle_frame.svg/200px-Circle_frame.svg.png" width="200" height="200" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/18/Circle_frame.svg/300px-Circle_frame.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/18/Circle_frame.svg/400px-Circle_frame.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div>
</div>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<p>Religion in Cape Verde (2010)<sup id="cite_ref-Pew_Forum.C2.A0.E2.80.94_Religion_in_Cape_Verde.282010.29_38-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pew_Forum.C2.A0.E2.80.94_Religion_in_Cape_Verde.282010.29-38"><span>[</span>38<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<div class="legend"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color:Green; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Catholic_Church" title="Catholic Church">Catholic Church</a> (78.7%)</div>
<div class="legend"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color:LimeGreen; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;Other Christian (10.4%)</div>
<div class="legend"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color:Yellow; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;Other or Non Religious (10.9%)</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Around 95% of the population are Christian. More than 85% of the population was nominally <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic" title="Roman Catholic" class="mw-redirect">Roman Catholic</a> in 2007.<sup id="cite_ref-rf_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-rf-39"><span>[</span>39<span>]</span></a></sup> For a minority of the population, Catholicism is <a href="/wiki/Syncretism" title="Syncretism">syncretized</a> with African influences.<sup id="cite_ref-factbook_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-factbook-40"><span>[</span>40<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>The largest <a href="/wiki/Protestant" title="Protestant" class="mw-redirect">Protestant</a> denomination is the <a href="/wiki/Church_of_the_Nazarene" title="Church of the Nazarene">Church of the Nazarene</a>; other groups include the <a href="/wiki/Seventh-day_Adventist_Church" title="Seventh-day Adventist Church">Seventh-day Adventist Church</a>, <a href="/wiki/The_Church_of_Jesus_Christ_of_Latter-day_Saints" title="The Church of Jesus Christ of Latter-day Saints">The Church of Jesus Christ of Latter-day Saints</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Assemblies_of_God" title="Assemblies of God">Assemblies of God</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Universal_Church_of_the_Kingdom_of_God" title="Universal Church of the Kingdom of God">Universal Church of the Kingdom of God</a>, and other <a href="/wiki/Pentecostal" title="Pentecostal" class="mw-redirect">Pentecostal</a> and <a href="/wiki/Evangelicalism" title="Evangelicalism">evangelical</a> groups.<sup id="cite_ref-rf_39-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-rf-39"><span>[</span>39<span>]</span></a></sup> There is a small <a href="/wiki/Islam" title="Islam">Muslim</a> community.<sup id="cite_ref-rf_39-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-rf-39"><span>[</span>39<span>]</span></a></sup> There were <a href="/wiki/History_of_the_Jews_in_Cape_Verde" title="History of the Jews in Cape Verde">Jewish</a> settlements on several islands.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41"><span>[</span>41<span>]</span></a></sup> The number of <a href="/wiki/Atheists" title="Atheists" class="mw-redirect">atheists</a> is estimated at less than 1% of the population.<sup id="cite_ref-rf_39-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-rf-39"><span>[</span>39<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Emigration_and_immigration">Emigration and immigration</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Cape_Verde&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Emigration and immigration">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote relarticle mainarticle">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Cape_Verdean_diaspora" title="Cape Verdean diaspora">Cape Verdean diaspora</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Gossiping.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Gossiping.jpg/250px-Gossiping.jpg" width="250" height="189" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Gossiping.jpg/375px-Gossiping.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Gossiping.jpg/500px-Gossiping.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1024" data-file-height="773" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Gossiping.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Local women on the island of <a href="/wiki/Santiago,_Cape_Verde" title="Santiago, Cape Verde">Santiago</a>.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Today, more Cape Verdeans live abroad than in Cape Verde itself, with significant emigrant<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42"><span>[</span>42<span>]</span></a></sup> Cape Verdean communities in the United States (500,000 Cape Verdeans descent, with a major concentration on the <a href="/wiki/New_England" title="New England">New England</a> coast from <a href="/wiki/Providence,_Rhode_Island" title="Providence, Rhode Island">Providence, Rhode Island</a>, to <a href="/wiki/New_Bedford,_Massachusetts" title="New Bedford, Massachusetts">New Bedford, Massachusetts</a>).</p>
<p>There are significant Cape Verde populations in Portugal (150,000), <a href="/wiki/Angola" title="Angola">Angola</a> (45,000), <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Tom%C3%A9_and_Pr%C3%ADncipe" title="S√£o Tom√© and Pr√≠ncipe">S√£o Tom√© and Pr√≠ncipe</a> (25,000), <a href="/wiki/Senegal" title="Senegal">Senegal</a> (25,000), the Netherlands (20,000, of which 15,000 are concentrated in <a href="/wiki/Rotterdam" title="Rotterdam">Rotterdam</a>), <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a> (25,000), Spain (12,500), Italy (10,000) <a href="/wiki/Luxembourg" title="Luxembourg">Luxembourg</a> (7,000) and Scandinavia (7,000). There is a Cape Verdean community in <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a> numbering 8,000. A large number of Cape Verdeans and people of Cape Verdean descent who emigrated before 1975 are not included in these statistics, because Cape Verdeans had Portuguese passports before 1975.</p>
<p>The Chinese make up a sizable and important segment of the immigrant population in Cape Verde. The immigrants from the nearby West Africa make up the majority of foreigners in the country. Over the last several years, a few thousands of Europeans and Latin Americans have settled in the country. On the islands, there are over 22,000 foreigners/naturalized Cape Verdeans living and working on a permanent basis.</p>
<p>Over the years, Cape Verde has increasingly become a net immigration country due to its relative high per capita income, political and social stability, and freedom.</p>
<p>In the United States, the children and grandchildren of the first immigrant waves became involved in the United States Army for centuries: in the Revolutionary War, Civil War, the First and Second World Wars, as well as the Korean and Vietnam Wars.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43"><span>[</span>43<span>]</span></a></sup> Cape Verdeans moved to places all over the world, from <a href="/wiki/Macau" title="Macau">Macau</a> to <a href="/wiki/Haiti" title="Haiti">Haiti</a> to Argentina to northern Europe.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44"><span>[</span>44<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Health">Health</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Cape_Verde&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Health">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote relarticle mainarticle">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Health_in_Cape_Verde" title="Health in Cape Verde">Health in Cape Verde</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><a href="/wiki/File:PraiaCentrodeSa%C3%BAde.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/86/PraiaCentrodeSa%C3%BAde.jpg/250px-PraiaCentrodeSa%C3%BAde.jpg" width="250" height="128" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/86/PraiaCentrodeSa%C3%BAde.jpg/375px-PraiaCentrodeSa%C3%BAde.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/86/PraiaCentrodeSa%C3%BAde.jpg/500px-PraiaCentrodeSa%C3%BAde.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1445" data-file-height="738" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:PraiaCentrodeSa%C3%BAde.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
A health clinic in a residential area of Praia.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The infant mortality rate in Cape Verde is 18.5 per 1,000 live births according to <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.un.cv/">[2]</a>, and the maternal mortality rate is 53.7 deaths per 100,000 live births. The AIDS prevalence rate is low: There are approximately 1,000 HIV/AIDS patients in the country, with just over half of these in <a href="/wiki/Praia" title="Praia">Praia</a> according to the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a>' HIV/AIDS 2013 report and the country's sexually transmitted diseases prevention bureau.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45"><span>[</span>45<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>At 75 years, Cape Verde (along with Tunisia and Libya) has the highest life expectancy across Africa, that is, 71 years for males and 79 years for females at birth in 2012 according to the <a href="/wiki/World_Bank" title="World Bank">World Bank</a> and <a href="/wiki/UNICEF" title="UNICEF">UNICEF</a>. There are six regional hospitals on five islands&#160;‚Äî Santiago (2), S√£o Vicente, S√£o Ant√£o, Fogo, and Sal. There are health centers, sanitation centers and a variety of private clinics located throughout the archipelago.</p>
<p>Cape Verde's population is among the healthiest in Africa. Since its independence, it has greatly improved its health indicators. Besides having been promoted to the group of "medium development" countries in 2007, leaving the <a href="/wiki/Least_developed_countries" title="Least developed countries" class="mw-redirect">least developed countries</a> category (which is only the second time it has happened to a country<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46"><span>[</span>46<span>]</span></a></sup>), is currently the <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_by_Human_Development_Index#Africa" title="List of countries by Human Development Index">9th best ranked</a> country in Africa in its <a href="/wiki/Human_Development_Index" title="Human Development Index">Human Development Index</a>.</p>
<p>The total expenditure for health was 4.8% of GDP (2011).</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Education">Education</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Cape_Verde&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Education">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote relarticle mainarticle">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Education_in_Cape_Verde" title="Education in Cape Verde">Education in Cape Verde</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Finalistas_do_jardim_infantil.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/24/Finalistas_do_jardim_infantil.jpg/250px-Finalistas_do_jardim_infantil.jpg" width="250" height="189" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/24/Finalistas_do_jardim_infantil.jpg/375px-Finalistas_do_jardim_infantil.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/24/Finalistas_do_jardim_infantil.jpg/500px-Finalistas_do_jardim_infantil.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1024" data-file-height="773" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Finalistas_do_jardim_infantil.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
A kindergarten graduation on Santiago island.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Although The Cape Verdean educational system is similar to the Portuguese system, over the years the local universities have been increasingly adopting the American educational system; for instance, all 10 existing universities in the country offer 4-year bachelor degree programs as opposed to 5-year bachelor degree programs that existed before 2010. Cape Verde has the second best educational system in Africa, after South Africa. Primary school education in Cape Verde is mandatory and free for children between the ages of 6 and 14 years.<sup id="cite_ref-ilab_47-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ilab-47"><span>[</span>47<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>In 2011, the net enrollment ratio for primary school was 85%.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48"><span>[</span>48<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ilab_47-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ilab-47"><span>[</span>47<span>]</span></a></sup> Approximately 90% of the total population over 15 years of age is literate, and roughly 25% of the population holds a college degree; 250 of these college graduates hold doctorate degrees in different academic fields. Textbooks have been made available to 90 percent of school children, and 98 percent of the teachers have attended in-service teacher training.<sup id="cite_ref-ilab_47-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ilab-47"><span>[</span>47<span>]</span></a></sup> Although most children have access to education, some problems remain.<sup id="cite_ref-ilab_47-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ilab-47"><span>[</span>47<span>]</span></a></sup> For example, there is insufficient spending on school materials, lunches, and books.<sup id="cite_ref-ilab_47-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ilab-47"><span>[</span>47<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>The total expenditure on education was 5.6% of GDP (2010). The mean years of schooling of adults over 25 years is 12.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Crime">Crime</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Cape_Verde&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Crime">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote">Further information: <a href="/wiki/Crime_in_Cape_Verde" title="Crime in Cape Verde">Crime in Cape Verde</a></div>
<p>Theft and <a href="/wiki/Burglary" title="Burglary">burglary</a> are common in Cape Verde especially in crowds, such as market places, festivals, and celebrations.<sup id="cite_ref-us_49-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-us-49"><span>[</span>49<span>]</span></a></sup> Often the perpetrators of these crimes are gangs of street children.<sup id="cite_ref-us_49-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-us-49"><span>[</span>49<span>]</span></a></sup> Murders are concentrated in the major population centres of Praia and Mindelo.<sup id="cite_ref-us_49-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-us-49"><span>[</span>49<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Culture">Culture</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Cape_Verde&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Culture">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote relarticle mainarticle">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Culture_of_Cape_Verde" title="Culture of Cape Verde">Culture of Cape Verde</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:237px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Morna_group.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Morna_group.jpg/235px-Morna_group.jpg" width="235" height="156" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Morna_group.jpg/353px-Morna_group.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Morna_group.jpg/470px-Morna_group.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="665" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Morna_group.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
A group playing <a href="/wiki/Morna_(music)" title="Morna (music)">morna</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:237px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Ch%C3%A3_das_Caldeiras-Musiciens.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Ch%C3%A3_das_Caldeiras-Musiciens.jpg/235px-Ch%C3%A3_das_Caldeiras-Musiciens.jpg" width="235" height="168" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Ch%C3%A3_das_Caldeiras-Musiciens.jpg/353px-Ch%C3%A3_das_Caldeiras-Musiciens.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Ch%C3%A3_das_Caldeiras-Musiciens.jpg/470px-Ch%C3%A3_das_Caldeiras-Musiciens.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3218" data-file-height="2306" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Ch%C3%A3_das_Caldeiras-Musiciens.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Musicians from <a href="/wiki/Ch%C3%A3_das_Caldeiras" title="Ch√£ das Caldeiras">Ch√£ das Caldeiras</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:162px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Mayra_Andrade.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/Mayra_Andrade.jpg/160px-Mayra_Andrade.jpg" width="160" height="176" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/Mayra_Andrade.jpg/240px-Mayra_Andrade.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/Mayra_Andrade.jpg/320px-Mayra_Andrade.jpg 2x" data-file-width="669" data-file-height="735" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Mayra_Andrade.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/Mayra_Andrade" title="Mayra Andrade">Mayra Andrade</a>, Cape Verdean singer who lives in Paris</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Cape Verdean social and cultural patterns are similar to those of rural Portugal .<sup id="cite_ref-pc_19-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pc-19"><span>[</span>19<span>]</span></a></sup> Football (Futebol) games and church activities are typical sources of social interaction and entertainment.<sup id="cite_ref-pc_19-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pc-19"><span>[</span>19<span>]</span></a></sup> The traditional walk around the pra√ßa (<a href="/wiki/Town_square" title="Town square">town square</a>) to meet friends is practised regularly in Cape Verde towns.<sup id="cite_ref-pc_19-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pc-19"><span>[</span>19<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Media">Media</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Cape_Verde&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Media">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote">Further information: <a href="/wiki/Media_of_Cape_Verde" title="Media of Cape Verde">Media of Cape Verde</a></div>
<p>In towns with electricity, television is available on two channels (Cape Verdean and Portuguese).<sup id="cite_ref-pc_19-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pc-19"><span>[</span>19<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Music">Music</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Cape_Verde&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Music">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote">Further information: <a href="/wiki/Music_of_Cape_Verde" title="Music of Cape Verde">Music of Cape Verde</a></div>
<p>Cape Verde music incorporates "African, <a href="/wiki/Lusitania" title="Lusitania">Lusitanian</a> and Brazilian influences."<sup id="cite_ref-manuel_50-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-manuel-50"><span>[</span>50<span>]</span></a></sup> Cape Verde's quintessential national music is the <i><a href="/wiki/Morna_(music)" title="Morna (music)">morna</a></i>, a melancholy and lyrical song form typically sung in <a href="/wiki/Cape_Verdean_Creole" title="Cape Verdean Creole">Cape Verdean Creole</a>. The most popular music genre after <i><a href="/wiki/Morna_(music)" title="Morna (music)">morna</a></i> is the <i><a href="/wiki/Coladeira" title="Coladeira">coladeira</a></i>, influenced by modern French Caribbean pop, followed by <i><a href="/wiki/Funan%C3%A1" title="Funan√°">funan√°</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Batuque_(music)" title="Batuque (music)" class="mw-redirect">batuque</a></i> music. Amongst the best known Cape Verdean singers worldwide are <a href="/wiki/Ildo_Lobo" title="Ildo Lobo">Ildo Lobo</a>, Nelson Freitas and <a href="/wiki/Ces%C3%A1ria_%C3%89vora" title="Ces√°ria √âvora">Ces√°ria √âvora</a> whose songs became a hallmark of the country and its culture.</p>
<p>There are also well known artists born to Cape Verdean parents who excelled themselves in the international music scene. Amongst these artists are jazz pianist <a href="/wiki/Horace_Silver" title="Horace Silver">Horace Silver</a>, <a href="/wiki/Duke_Ellington" title="Duke Ellington">Duke Ellington</a>'s saxophonist <a href="/wiki/Paul_Gonsalves" title="Paul Gonsalves">Paul Gonsalves</a>, <a href="/wiki/Te%C3%B3filo_Chantre" title="Te√≥filo Chantre">Te√≥filo Chantre</a>, <a href="/wiki/Paul_Pena" title="Paul Pena">Paul Pena</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Tavares_(group)" title="Tavares (group)">Tavares</a> brothers and singer <a href="/wiki/Lura_(musician)" title="Lura (musician)" class="mw-redirect">Lura</a>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Dance">Dance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Cape_Verde&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Dance">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Dance forms include the soft dance <i>morna</i>, the extreme sensuality of <i><a href="/wiki/Coladeira" title="Coladeira">coladeira</a></i> including the modernized version called <i><a href="/wiki/Cabo_love" title="Cabo love" class="mw-redirect">Cabo love</a></i> (similar to the <a href="/wiki/Zouk" title="Zouk">zouk</a> from <a href="/wiki/Guadeloupe" title="Guadeloupe">Guadeloupe</a>), the <i><a href="/wiki/Funan%C3%A1" title="Funan√°">Funan√°</a></i> (a sensual mixed Portuguese and African dance), and the <i><a href="/wiki/Batuque_(music)" title="Batuque (music)" class="mw-redirect">Batuque</a></i> dance.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Literature">Literature</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Cape_Verde&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Literature">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Cape Verdean literature is one of the richest of <a href="/wiki/Lusophone" title="Lusophone">Lusophone</a> Africa. Famous poets include Paulino Vieira, Manuel de Novas, Sergio Frusoni, Eug√©nio Tavares, and B. L√©za, and famous authors include <a href="/wiki/Baltasar_Lopes_da_Silva" title="Baltasar Lopes da Silva">Baltasar Lopes da Silva</a>, Ant√≥nio Aur√©lio Gon√ßalves, <a href="/wiki/Manuel_Lopes" title="Manuel Lopes">Manuel Lopes</a>, <a href="/wiki/Orlanda_Amar%C3%ADlis" title="Orlanda Amar√≠lis">Orlanda Amar√≠lis</a>, <a href="/wiki/Henrique_Teixeira_de_Sousa" title="Henrique Teixeira de Sousa">Henrique Teixeira de Sousa</a>, <a href="/wiki/Arm%C3%A9nio_Vieira" title="Arm√©nio Vieira">Arm√©nio Vieira</a>, Kaubverdianu Dambar√°, Dr. Az√°gua, and <a href="/wiki/Germano_Almeida" title="Germano Almeida">Germano Almeida</a>.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Cuisine">Cuisine</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Cape_Verde&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Cuisine">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The Cape Verde diet is mostly based on fish and staple foods like <a href="/wiki/Maize" title="Maize">corn</a> and <a href="/wiki/Rice" title="Rice">rice</a>. Vegetables available during most of the year are <a href="/wiki/Potato" title="Potato">potatoes</a>, <a href="/wiki/Onion" title="Onion">onions</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tomato" title="Tomato">tomatoes</a>, <a href="/wiki/Manioc" title="Manioc" class="mw-redirect">manioc</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cabbage" title="Cabbage">cabbage</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kale" title="Kale">kale</a>, and dried <a href="/wiki/Bean" title="Bean">beans</a>. Fruits such as <a href="/wiki/Banana" title="Banana">bananas</a> and <a href="/wiki/Papaya" title="Papaya">papayas</a> are available year-round, while others like <a href="/wiki/Mango" title="Mango">mangoes</a> and <a href="/wiki/Avocado" title="Avocado">avocados</a> are seasonal.<sup id="cite_ref-pc_19-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pc-19"><span>[</span>19<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>A popular dish served in Cape Verde is <a href="/wiki/Cachupa" title="Cachupa">Cachupa</a>, a slow cooked <a href="/wiki/Stew" title="Stew">stew</a> of corn (hominy), beans, and fish or meat. A common appetizer is the <a href="/wiki/Pastel" title="Pastel">pastel</a> which is a pastry shell filled with fish or meat that is then fried.<sup id="cite_ref-pc_19-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pc-19"><span>[</span>19<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sports">Sports</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Cape_Verde&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Sports">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Cape Verde is famous for wave sailing (a type of windsurfing) and <a href="/wiki/Kitesurfing" title="Kitesurfing">kiteboarding</a>. Josh Angulo, a Hawaiian and 2009 PWA Wave World Champion, has done much to promote the archipelago as a <a href="/wiki/Windsurfing" title="Windsurfing">windsurfing</a> destination. Cape Verde is now his adopted country. Mitu Monteiro, a local kitesurfer, was the 2008 <a href="/wiki/International_Kiteboarding_Association#Wave_Riding" title="International Kiteboarding Association">Kite Surfing World Champion</a> in the wave discipline.</p>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Cape_Verde_national_football_team" title="Cape Verde national football team">Cape Verde national football team</a>, nicknamed either the <i>Tubar√µes Azuis</i> (Blue Sharks) or <i>Crioulos</i> (Creoles), is the national team of Cape Verde and is controlled by the <a href="/wiki/Federa%C3%A7%C3%A3o_Caboverdiana_de_Futebol" title="Federa√ß√£o Caboverdiana de Futebol">Federa√ß√£o Caboverdiana de Futebol</a>. The team has played at two <a href="/wiki/Africa_Cup_of_Nations" title="Africa Cup of Nations">Africa Cup of Nations</a>, in <a href="/wiki/2013_Africa_Cup_of_Nations" title="2013 Africa Cup of Nations">2013</a> and <a href="/wiki/2015_Africa_Cup_of_Nations" title="2015 Africa Cup of Nations">2015</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51"><span>[</span>51<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>The country has competed at every <a href="/wiki/Summer_Olympics" title="Summer Olympics" class="mw-redirect">Summer Olympics</a> since 1996.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Transport">Transport</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Cape_Verde&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Transport">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote relarticle mainarticle">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Transport_in_Cape_Verde" title="Transport in Cape Verde">Transport in Cape Verde</a></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ports">Ports</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Cape_Verde&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Ports">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Ports and harbors: Mindelo on S√£o Vicente is the main port for cruise liners and the terminus for the ferry service to Santo Ant√£o. Praia on Santiago is a main hub for local ferry services to other islands. Palmeira on Sal supplies fuel for the main airport on the island, Am√≠lcar Cabral International Airport, and is important for the hotel construction taking place on the island. Porto Novo on Santo Ant√£o is the only source for imports and exports of produce from the island as well as passenger traffic since the closure of the airstrip at Ponta do Sol.</p>
<p>There are smaller harbors, essentially single jetties at Tarrafal on S√£o Nicolau, Sal Rei on Boa Vista, Vila do Maio (Porto Ingl√™s) on Maio, S√£o Filipe on Fogo and Furna on Brava. These act as terminals for the inter-island ferry services, which carry both freight and passengers. The pier at Santa Maria on Sal used by both fishing and dive boats has been rehabilitated.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Airports">Airports</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Cape_Verde&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Airports">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Seven operational in 2014&#160;‚Äî 4 international and 3 domestic.<br />
Two non-operational, one on Brava and the other on Santo Ant√£o, closed for safety reasons.</p>
